Installed 09/06/2026 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/178013/) (Environmental) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/1704/images/178013/178013-1776769579-1592745484.jpg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By DimitriDark for Skyrim Special Edition (Default)

A patch for Dynamic Wind and Aspens Ablaze Animated Branches that includes a configurable .json file for each of the three aspen tree types. This patch allows for both mods to be used together and for aspens to behave normally in the wind rather than sway madly in all directions.

### FUS RO DON&#39;T - PushActorAway Crash Prevention Script Tweak 1.0.0

Installed 16/05/2026 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/57816/) (Bug Fixes) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/1704/images/57816/57816-1635830297-1600341885.png" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By celadoneiron for Skyrim Special Edition (Default)

If the game tries to throw an NPC with PushActorAway, but the NPC hasn't fully loaded in yet, the game will crash. This mod adds checks to two vanilla scripts to make sure the caster and target both have their 3D fully loaded before trying to use PushActorAway, which stops the NPC from being thrown if the game isn't ready and prevents the crash.

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/1704/images/2241-0-1478040128.jpg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By Kotep for Skyrim Special Edition (Default)

Get to and from all hold capitals by carriage.  Carriages now leave from Dawnstar, Falkreath, Morthal and Winterhold.

### Hearthfire Carriage Destinations 1.03 1.03

Installed 28/06/2026 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/2647/) (Cheats and God items) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/1704/images/2647-0-1478205867.jpg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By tortugapir8 for Skyrim Special Edition (Default)

A simple extension to add the 3 player homes in Hearthfires (Heljarchen, Lakeview, and Windstad) as destinations to all existing carriages (including those at the player homes as well).

### Stormfang - Main Replacer 1.1

Installed 28/06/2026 from [Nexus Mods](https://www.nexusmods.com/skyrimspecialedition/mods/24505/) (Weapons) 

<img src="https://staticdelivery.nexusmods.com/mods/1704/images/24505/24505-1598191920-1582590497.jpeg" alt="mod-image" height="350" />

> By Vilidran for Skyrim Special Edition (Default)

A model replacer for the unique weapon "Stormfang" which can be found in Solstheim. Also adds a craftable unenchanted version at the forge after finishing the quest "Lost Legacy".
